12) ููุงุท ุชุตููโฺฏุฑ ููู (Design Decisions & Tradeoffs)

  • **Referral on-chain vs off-chain**: on-chain ุดูุงูโุชุฑ ุงุณุชุ ุงูุง ฺฏุณโุจูููโุชุฑ ูุณุช. ูพุดููุงุฏ: ุซุจุช referer on-chain ููุท ฺฉ ุจุงุฑุ ู ุชูุฒุน ููฺฉุงู/ุจฺ ุจุฑุง ุตุฑููโุฌู ุฏุฑ ฺฏุณ.
  • **Upgradeable vs Immutable**: ุงููุช ู ุงุนุชูุงุฏ ุจุง immutability ุจูุชุฑ ุงุณุชุ ุงูุง ูุงุจูุช ุงุตูุงุญ ุจุง Proxy ุจุฑุง ูุงฺููโูุง ฺฉูโุฑุณฺฉ ูพุดููุงุฏ ูโุดูุฏ (ุชุญุช Timelock + MultiSig).
  • **Auto-Liquidity**: ูุงุฒู ุจุฑุง ูพุงุฏุงุฑ ููุช ุงูุง ุจุงุฏ ุจุง ูุญุฏูุฏุช ู lock LP ููุฑุงู ุจุงุดุฏ ุชุง ุณูุกุงุณุชูุงุฏู ูุดูุฏ.

13) ูุซุงูโูุง ฺฉุฏ (ูููููู ุดุจูโฺฉุฏ Solidity ุจุฑุง _transfer)

(ุจุฑุง ูุฑุฌุน ุณุฑุน ููุฒ)

function _transfer(address sender, address recipient, uint256 amount) internal override {
    if(isExcludedFromFee[sender] || isExcludedFromFee[recipient]) {
        super._transfer(sender, recipient, amount);
        return;
    }
    uint256 taxAmount = amount * taxPercent / 100;
    uint256 net = amount - taxAmount;

    uint256 liquidityShare = taxAmount * liquidityPercent / 100;
    uint256 marketingShare = taxAmount * marketingPercent / 100;
    uint256 referralShare = taxAmount - liquidityShare - marketingShare;

    // collect tax in contract
    super._transfer(sender, address(this), taxAmount);

    // send marketing
    if(marketingShare>0) super._transfer(address(this), marketingWallet, marketingShare);

    // referral distribution (simple on-the-fly)
    address r1 = referer[recipient] != address(0) ? referer[recipient] : referer[sender];
    if(r1 != address(0) && referralShare>0) {
        uint256 r1Share = referralShare * 50 / 100; // 50% to level1
        super._transfer(address(this), r1, r1Share);
        uint256 rest = referralShare - r1Share;
        if(rest>0) super._transfer(address(this), referralPool, rest);
    } else {
        super._transfer(address(this), referralPool, referralShare);
    }

    // final transfer
    super._transfer(sender, recipient, net);
}

> ุชูุฌู: ุงู ููุท ุฌูุช ุจุฑุฑุณ ููุทู ุงุณุชุ ูุณุฎู ููุง ุจุงุฏ ุจููู ฺฏุณุ ููุงูู ุฏุฑ ุจุฑุงุจุฑ reentrancy ู ุฏุงุฑุง ููุฒ ุจุงุดุฏ.

14) ุฑุณฺฉโูุง ูู ูฺู ู ุชูุตูโูุง ุชฺฉูู

  • **Edge case:** ุชูฺฉูโูุง ฺฉู ุฏุฑ ุงุถุงูู ฺฉุฑุฏู liquidity ูุงุฒููุฏ ฺฺฉโูุง ุฎุงุต (ูุซูุงู token tax) ุฑุง ุจุฑุฑุณ ฺฉูุฏ ุชุง ุญููู ุชูฺฉูโุจูุงุฏ ุงุฌุงุฏ ูุดูุฏ.

12) ููุงุท ุชุตููโฺฏุฑ ููู (Design Decisions & Tradeoffs)

  • **Tax on transfer**: ุณุงุฏู ู ฺฉุงุฑุง ูู ูุฒูู ฺฏุณ ุจุฑุง ูููุฏุฑูุง ุฏุงุฑุฏุ ุจุงุฏ ุฏุฑุตุฏ ูุนููู (ูุซูุงู 3%) ุจุงุดุฏ.
  • **Referral on-chain vs off-chain**: on-chain ุดูุงูโุชุฑ ุงุณุชุ ุงูุง ฺฏุณโุจูููโุชุฑ ูุณุช. ูพุดููุงุฏ: ุซุจุช referer on-chain ููุท ฺฉ ุจุงุฑุ ู ุชูุฒุน ููฺฉุงู/ุจฺ ุจุฑุง ุตุฑููโุฌู ุฏุฑ ฺฏุณ.
  • **Upgradeable vs Immutable**: ุงููุช ู ุงุนุชูุงุฏ ุจุง immutability ุจูุชุฑ ุงุณุชุ ุงูุง ูุงุจูุช ุงุตูุงุญ ุจุง Proxy ุจุฑุง ูุงฺููโูุง ฺฉูโุฑุณฺฉ ูพุดููุงุฏ ูโุดูุฏ (ุชุญุช Timelock + MultiSig).
  • **Auto-Liquidity**: ูุงุฒู ุจุฑุง ูพุงุฏุงุฑ ููุช ุงูุง ุจุงุฏ ุจุง ูุญุฏูุฏุช ู lock LP ููุฑุงู ุจุงุดุฏ ุชุง ุณูุกุงุณุชูุงุฏู ูุดูุฏ.

13) ูุซุงูโูุง ฺฉุฏ (ูููููู ุดุจูโฺฉุฏ Solidity ุจุฑุง _transfer)

(ุจุฑุง ูุฑุฌุน ุณุฑุน ููุฒ)

function _transfer(address sender, address recipient, uint256 amount) internal override {
    if(isExcludedFromFee[sender] || isExcludedFromFee[recipient]) {
        super._transfer(sender, recipient, amount);
        return;
    }
    uint256 taxAmount = amount * taxPercent / 100;
    uint256 net = amount - taxAmount;

    uint256 liquidityShare = taxAmount * liquidityPercent / 100;
    uint256 marketingShare = taxAmount * marketingPercent / 100;
    uint256 referralShare = taxAmount - liquidityShare - marketingShare;

    // collect tax in contract
    super._transfer(sender, address(this), taxAmount);

    // send marketing
    if(marketingShare>0) super._transfer(address(this), marketingWallet, marketingShare);

    // referral distribution (simple on-the-fly)
    address r1 = referer[recipient] != address(0) ? referer[recipient] : referer[sender];
    if(r1 != address(0) && referralShare>0) {
        uint256 r1Share = referralShare * 50 / 100; // 50% to level1
        super._transfer(address(this), r1, r1Share);
        uint256 rest = referralShare - r1Share;
        if(rest>0) super._transfer(address(this), referralPool, rest);
    } else {
        super._transfer(address(this), referralPool, referralShare);
    }

    // final transfer
    super._transfer(sender, recipient, net);
}

> ุชูุฌู: ุงู ููุท ุฌูุช ุจุฑุฑุณ ููุทู ุงุณุชุ ูุณุฎู ููุง ุจุงุฏ ุจููู ฺฏุณุ ููุงูู ุฏุฑ ุจุฑุงุจุฑ reentrancy ู ุฏุงุฑุง ููุฒ ุจุงุดุฏ.

14) ุฑุณฺฉโูุง ูู ูฺู ู ุชูุตูโูุง ุชฺฉูู

  • **Edge case:** ุชูฺฉูโูุง ฺฉู ุฏุฑ ุงุถุงูู ฺฉุฑุฏู liquidity ูุงุฒููุฏ ฺฺฉโูุง ุฎุงุต (ูุซูุงู token tax) ุฑุง ุจุฑุฑุณ ฺฉูุฏ ุชุง ุญููู ุชูฺฉูโุจูุงุฏ ุงุฌุงุฏ ูุดูุฏ.
